            <h2 class="entry-title display-3" itemprop="headline">
             <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/interview-crazetalks-north-african-fashions-it-girl/" title="Interview: CrazeTalks – North African Fashion’s It-Girl">

             </a>
            </h2>
            <div class="df-post-on">
             <time class="entry-published updated" datetime="2018-07-23T10:38:31+00:00" title="Monday, July 23, 2018, 10:38 am">

           <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/interview-crazetalks-north-african-fashions-it-girl/">
            <img alt="Sofia El Arabi" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" height="850" sizes="(max-width: 1280px) 100vw, 1280px" src="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Photo-1.png" srcset="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Photo-1.png 1280w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Photo-1-300x199.png 300w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Photo-1-768x510.png 768w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Photo-1-1024x680.png 1024w" width="1280"/>
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="entry-content" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Published on Afrocraze.com in July 19, 2018 Featured in Vogue USA, Vogue Arabia, Huffington Post, Velvet Magazine, and ( so ) many more publications, Sofia El Arabi has undoubtedly made a name for herself in the fashion world. With a personal style that can only be described as, a queen of the desert meets Emmanuelle …

            <h2 class="entry-title display-3" itemprop="headline">
             <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/eid-agadir-exploring-moroccan-souks-culture-fashion/" title="Eid in Agadir: Exploring Moroccan Souks, Culture and Fashion">
              Eid in Agadir: Exploring Moroccan Souks, Culture and Fashion
             </a>
            </h2>
            <div class="df-post-on">
             <time class="entry-published updated" datetime="2018-07-18T10:33:15+00:00" title="Wednesday, July 18, 2018, 10:33 am">
              <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/2018/07/18/">

          <div class="featured-media filter_bw">
           <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/eid-agadir-exploring-moroccan-souks-culture-fashion/">
            <img alt="Agadir" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" height="1076" sizes="(max-width: 2326px) 100vw, 2326px" src="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Screen-Shot-2018-07-18-at-11.28.55.png" srcset="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Screen-Shot-2018-07-18-at-11.28.55.png 2326w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Screen-Shot-2018-07-18-at-11.28.55-300x139.png 300w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Screen-Shot-2018-07-18-at-11.28.55-768x355.png 768w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/Screen-Shot-2018-07-18-at-11.28.55-1024x474.png 1024w" width="2326"/>

           <p>
            Published on Afrocraze.com in June 30, 2018 Celebrating Eid in Agadir, Morocco. We explored Moroccan souks, where fashion &amp; celebration intersect, in search of the perfect outfit for this special day. In collaboration with Kaftan Mag. Music by Brahim Fribgane.

            <h2 class="entry-title display-3" itemprop="headline">
             <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/who-made-my-clothes/" title="Who made my clothes ?">
              Who made my clothes ?
             </a>
            </h2>
            <div class="df-post-on">
             <time class="entry-published updated" datetime="2018-06-19T10:35:47+00:00" title="Tuesday, June 19, 2018, 10:35 am">
              <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/2018/06/19/">
               <meta content="June 19, 2018" itemprop="datePublished"/>
               June 19, 2018
              </a>
             </time>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="featured-media filter_bw">
           <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/who-made-my-clothes/">
            <img alt="“Who made my clothes?”" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" height="1390" sizes="(max-width: 2048px) 100vw, 2048px" src="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/Fashion-Revolution-Morocco.jpg" srcset="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/Fashion-Revolution-Morocco.jpg 2048w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/Fashion-Revolution-Morocco-300x204.jpg 300w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/Fashion-Revolution-Morocco-768x521.jpg 768w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/Fashion-Revolution-Morocco-1024x695.jpg 1024w" width="2048"/>
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="entry-content" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Published on Afrocraze.com in May 29, 2018 A few weeks ago on AfroCraze, we talked about ethical fashion on the African landscape; “Zooming in on the practice of ethical fashion that is sourced and produced on the African continent, we at AfroCraze believe that the true embodiment of ethical fashion goes beyond not doing harm. …

            <h2 class="entry-title display-3" itemprop="headline">
             <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/moroccan-mystery-really-kaftan/" title="Moroccan Mystery: What Really is a Kaftan?">
              Moroccan Mystery: What Really is a Kaftan?
             </a>
            </h2>
            <div class="df-post-on">
             <time class="entry-published updated" datetime="2018-06-19T10:01:13+00:00" title="Tuesday, June 19, 2018, 10:01 am">
              <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/2018/06/19/">
               <meta content="June 19, 2018" itemprop="datePublished"/>
               June 19, 2018
              </a>
             </time>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="featured-media filter_bw">
           <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/moroccan-mystery-really-kaftan/">
            <img alt="Moroccan kaftan" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" height="2219" sizes="(max-width: 2800px) 100vw, 2800px" src="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/rad-kaftan_Fotor-e1529402452168.jpg" srcset="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/rad-kaftan_Fotor-e1529402452168.jpg 2800w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/rad-kaftan_Fotor-e1529402452168-300x238.jpg 300w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/rad-kaftan_Fotor-e1529402452168-768x609.jpg 768w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/rad-kaftan_Fotor-e1529402452168-1024x812.jpg 1024w" width="2800"/>
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="entry-content" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Published on Afrocraze.com in March 30, 2018 What is a kaftan, really? In what garment “box” should we put it? Dresses? Outerwear? Formal? Casual? Even the Moroccan that I am, can get confused at times. However, one thing I know for sure, is that I am “Caftan with a “K” team”, all the way. Ka …

            Published on Afrocraze.com in March 30, 2018 “When Yves Saint Laurent discovered Marrakech in 1966, he was so moved by the place that he decided to buy a house and regularly go back there. It feels perfectly natural, fifty years later, to build a museum dedicated to his oeuvre, which was so inspired by this …

            <h2 class="entry-title display-3" itemprop="headline">
             <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/spring-fashion-basics/" title="Spring fashion basics">
              Spring fashion basics
             </a>
            </h2>
            <div class="df-post-on">
             <time class="entry-published updated" datetime="2018-03-21T11:06:01+00:00" title="Wednesday, March 21, 2018, 11:06 am">
              <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/2018/03/21/">
               <meta content="March 21, 2018" itemprop="datePublished"/>
               March 21, 2018
              </a>
             </time>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="featured-media filter_bw">
           <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/spring-fashion-basics/">
            <img alt="Spring fashion" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" height="3456" sizes="(max-width: 5184px) 100vw, 5184px" src="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/IMG_1669.jpg" srcset="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/IMG_1669.jpg 5184w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/IMG_1669-300x200.jpg 300w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/IMG_1669-768x512.jpg 768w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/IMG_1669-1024x683.jpg 1024w" width="5184"/>
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="entry-content" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Happy Spring everyone! Finally! No offense to winter, but I’m so done with knits, sweaters, and coats! Bring on light layers, and spring fashion basics. I have here a selection of clothing pieces, mostly basics (Dah! It’s me, the basics’ w****), that will make for the perfect spring wardrobe.
           </p>

            <h2 class="entry-title display-3" itemprop="headline">
             <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/come-to-marrakech-with-me/" title="Come to Marrakech with me">
              Come to Marrakech with me
             </a>
            </h2>
            <div class="df-post-on">
             <time class="entry-published updated" datetime="2018-03-14T11:39:47+00:00" title="Wednesday, March 14, 2018, 11:39 am">

           <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/come-to-marrakech-with-me/">

            <h2 class="entry-title display-3" itemprop="headline">
             <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/follow-youtube-channel/" title="Follow my Youtube channel">
              Follow my Youtube channel
             </a>
            </h2>
            <div class="df-post-on">
             <time class="entry-published updated" datetime="2018-03-01T14:37:47+00:00" title="Thursday, March 1, 2018, 2:37 pm">
              <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/2018/03/01/">
               <meta content="March 1, 2018" itemprop="datePublished"/>
               March 1, 2018
              </a>
             </time>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="featured-media filter_bw">
           <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/follow-youtube-channel/">
            <img alt="Youtube channel" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" height="1160" sizes="(max-width: 2060px) 100vw, 2060px" src="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/Screen-Shot-2018-02-24-at-194534-copy.jpg" srcset="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/Screen-Shot-2018-02-24-at-194534-copy.jpg 2060w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/Screen-Shot-2018-02-24-at-194534-copy-300x169.jpg 300w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/Screen-Shot-2018-02-24-at-194534-copy-768x432.jpg 768w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/Screen-Shot-2018-02-24-at-194534-copy-1024x577.jpg 1024w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/Screen-Shot-2018-02-24-at-194534-copy-1140x641.jpg 1140w" width="2060"/>

          <div class="entry-content" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            This is not an order, but a mere suggestion! In this video, I explain in all honesty the reasons behind me; normally a shy person, starting a Youtube channel. I also tell you why I think you would enjoy watching my videos.
           </p>

            <h2 class="entry-title display-3" itemprop="headline">
             <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/tips-better-instagram-feed/" title="Tips for a better Instagram feed">
              Tips for a better Instagram feed
             </a>
            </h2>
            <div class="df-post-on">
             <time class="entry-published updated" datetime="2018-02-05T12:21:03+00:00" title="Monday, February 5, 2018, 12:21 pm">
              <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/2018/02/05/">
               <meta content="February 5, 2018" itemprop="datePublished"/>
               February 5, 2018
              </a>
             </time>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="featured-media filter_bw">
           <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/tips-better-instagram-feed/">
            <img alt="Better Instagram feed" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" height="2340" sizes="(max-width: 3992px) 100vw, 3992px" src="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/better-Instagram-Collage.jpg" srcset="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/better-Instagram-Collage.jpg 3992w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/better-Instagram-Collage-300x176.jpg 300w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/better-Instagram-Collage-768x450.jpg 768w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/better-Instagram-Collage-1024x600.jpg 1024w" width="3992"/>
           </a>

          <div class="entry-content" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            In case you haven’t figured it out yet, beautiful instagram feeds have become #lifegoals. And today, I’m here to tell you that it doesn’t take that much, to up you insta game, and get a better Instagram feed.
           </p>

            <h2 class="entry-title display-3" itemprop="headline">
             <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/dressed-winter-kaftan-layering/" title="Dressed up winter kaftan layering">
              Dressed up winter kaftan layering
             </a>
            </h2>
            <div class="df-post-on">
             <time class="entry-published updated" datetime="2018-02-01T19:00:14+00:00" title="Thursday, February 1, 2018, 7:00 pm">
              <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/2018/02/01/">
               <meta content="February 1, 2018" itemprop="datePublished"/>
               February 1, 2018
              </a>
             </time>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="featured-media filter_bw">
           <a href="http://www.kaftanmag.com/dressed-winter-kaftan-layering/">
            <img alt="Dressed up winter" class="attachment-full size-full wp-post-image" height="3456" sizes="(max-width: 5184px) 100vw, 5184px" src="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/IMG_9322.jpg" srcset="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/IMG_9322.jpg 5184w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/IMG_9322-300x200.jpg 300w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/IMG_9322-768x512.jpg 768w, http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/IMG_9322-1024x683.jpg 1024w" width="5184"/>
           </a>
          </div>
          <div class="entry-content" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Winter or not, cold or not, nothing can stop me from wearing my dear kaftans. Well, actually to be honest, wearing a kaftan during winter only gives me an (extra) excuse to layer!! I LOVE layering, in case I haven’t said that enough, in previous posts! And when you mix a kaftan, with layering, the …

             Continue Reading
             <i class="ion-ios-arrow-thin-right">
             </i>
            </a>
           </p>

         <div class="widget about-widget" id="about-widget-1">
          <h4>
           <span>
            About Me
           </span>
          </h4>
          <div class="about-content aligncenter">
           <div class="about-avatar">
            <img alt="About Me" src="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/03/DSC_9238-1024x678.jpg"/>
           </div>
           <div class="content-wrap">
            <p>
             “Marhaba”.
 
 My name is Souad El Mghari, born and raised in the “adorable” Moroccan town of Agadir, Fashion has always been a passion of mine. Even before I was at the age of realizing it.
 
 My first memory as a child is arguing with my mom on a school morning about what I should wear. And I should add, I won that argument. From that day on, I dressed myself (and others for that matter).
 
 Today, the editor-in-chief of a women’s magazine in Morocco, a freelance stylist, and fashion editor, it was a long way here, and I won’t have had it any other way.
 
 This blog is a sort of journal for my creativity, a reflection of me; my esthetic, interests, take on things that I come across. Be it fashion trends, beauty products, or lifestyle subjects. Hence, its name “Kaftan Mag”. “Kaftan” in hommage to my heritage, my roots, my pride; aka Morocco, and “Mag” as a reflection of my passion and love for media and publishing.
             <img alt="signature" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-114" src="http://www.kaftanmag.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/Souad_El_Mghari_Signature.png"/>
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <a href="https://twitter.com/kaftanmag" target="_blank">
               <i class="fa fa-twitter">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://www.facebook.com/runninginakaftan/" target="_blank">
               <i class="fa fa-facebook">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://www.instagram.com/souad.kaftanmag/" target="_blank">
               <i class="fa fa-instagram">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/kaftanmag/" target="_blank">
               <i class="fa fa-pinterest">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
